<style>
	@media (max-width: 768px) and (min-width: 600px)
	{
		#News .news-preview
		{
			width: 50%;
			display: block;
			float: left;
		}
		
		#News .news-preview .news-text
		{
			flex: auto;
		}

					#News #news-ident-1,
			#News #news-ident-2
			{
				display: block;
			}
		
			#News #news-ident-3,
			#News #news-ident-4,
			#News #news-ident-5,
			#News #news-ident-6
			{
				display: none;
			}
			}
	
	@media (max-width: 600px)
	{
		#News .news-preview
		{
			width: 100%;
			display: block;
			float: left;
		}
		
		#News .news-preview .news-text
		{
			flex: auto;
		}

					#News #news-ident-1
			{
				display: block;
			}
		
			#News #news-ident-2,
			#News #news-ident-3,
			#News #news-ident-4,
			#News #news-ident-5,
			#News #news-ident-6
			{
				display: none;
			}
			}
</style>
<script>
	var aktSubPage = 1;
	
		
	function loadNewsList(lnk, direction) {
		searchStr = 'pageNews=';
		pos = lnk.indexOf(searchStr);
		page = lnk.substring(pos+searchStr.length, lnk.length);
		
		doAjax = true;
		
		if($(window).width() <= 768)
		{
			pages = 3;
			display = 2;
			
			if($(window).width() <= 600)
			{
				pages = 6;
				display = 1;
			}
			
			if(direction == 'next' && aktSubPage < pages)
			{
				doAjax = false;
				aktSubPage = aktSubPage + 1;
			}
			
			if(direction == 'prev' && page == 0 && aktSubPage == 1)
			{
				return false;
			}
			else if(direction == 'prev' && aktSubPage > 1)
			{
				doAjax = false;
				aktSubPage = aktSubPage - 1;
			}
		}
		
		if(! doAjax)
		{
			//Pfeile manipulieren
			if(page == 0 && aktSubPage == 1)
			{
				$('#News .Backwa span').each(function() {
					$(this).addClass('disabled');
				});
			}
			else
			{
				$('#News .Backwa span').each(function() {
					$(this).removeClass('disabled');
				});
			}
			
			$('.news-preview').each(function() {
				$(this).css('display', 'none');
			});
		
			startNews = ((aktSubPage-1) * display) + 1;
			endNews = startNews + (display - 1);

			for(i=startNews; i<=endNews; i++)
			{
				$('#news-ident-'+i).each(function() {
					$(this).css('display', 'block');
				});
			}

			return false;
		}

		if(direction == 'next')
		{
			aktSubPage = 1;
		}
		else
		{
			aktSubPage = page;
		}
		
		$("#newsContainer").load(
			"/ajax/news_list.php",
			{
				cmsBereich: '',
				styleKeyword: '',
				editMode: '',
				page: page,
				direction: direction,
			}
		);

		return false;
	}
</script>

<div id="News">

<div class="col colTxt">
<h3><strong>Newsletter der Stadt Oberhausen</strong></h3>

<p>Donnerstag ist Newsletter-Tag! Bekommen Sie schon unseren w&ouml;chentlichen Newsletter mit allen aktuellen Ereignissen, Baustellenmeldungen und Terminen in und aus Oberhausen?</p>

<p>Behalten Sie die wichtigsten Infos der Woche auf einen Blick und verpassen Sie&nbsp;nichts, was in Ihrer Stadt geschieht.&nbsp;</p>

<p>Wenn nicht, abonnieren Sie jetzt unseren Newsletter! Hier geht es zur <a class="arrowDbl" href="/newsletter.php" title="Newsletteranmeldung öffnet im selben Fenster.">Anmeldung</a>.</p>
</div>

<div class="col-sm-auto mb-sm-0 mb-1 colImg">

<div class="contentField">
<div class="row">
<div class="col colTxt">
<h3><strong><a class="arrowDbl" href="http://www.oberhausen-tourismus.de/service/broschueren/" target="_blank" title="Link zur Seite der Tourist Information öffnet in neuem Fenster">Oberhausen: Reisemagazin 2026</a></strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;</h3>

<p>Genau das Richtige f&uuml;r eine Tour mit Freunden oder der Familie: Die&nbsp;TOURIST INFORMATION Oberhausen&nbsp;hat ein neues Besucher- und&nbsp;Reisemagazin&nbsp;f&uuml;r das Jahr 2026 aufgelegt. Die kostenlose Brosch&uuml;re&nbsp;mit den wichtigsten Infos zu den Saisonhighlights ist eine unentbehrliche Planungshilfe f&uuml;r alle G&auml;ste der Stadt.</p>
</div>

<div class="col-sm-auto mb-sm-0 mb-1 colImg">
<figure><img alt="Titel der Broschüre DAS REISEMAGAZIN" src="/bilder/banner/reisemagazin-2026-530px.jpg" /></figure>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<script src="/dist/js/app.js?v=1784159867"></script>
<script>
	var debounce = null;
	function search_suggestion(elem, block)
	{
   		clearTimeout(debounce);

   		debounce = setTimeout(function(){
      		search_suggestion_do_search(elem, block);
   		}, 500);
	}
	
	function search_suggestion_do_search(elem, block)
	{
		searchString = $(elem).val();
		if(searchString.length >= 3)
		{
			$.ajax({
				method: "POST",
				url: "/ajax/search_suggestion.php",
				data: { 
					searchString: searchString,
				}
			}).done(function(data) {
				data = $.parseJSON(data);
				targetElem = $('#' + block);

				targetElem.html('');
				targetElem.css('display', 'none');
				text = '';
				if(data.length > 0)
				{
					text += '<ul>';
					$.each(data, function(i, item) {
						text += '<li><a href="'+item.link+'" target="_self">'+item.name+'</a></li>';
					});
					text += '</ul>';

					targetElem.html(text);
					targetElem.css('display', 'block');
				}
			});
		}
	}
</script>


<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

		const logoutButton = document.getElementById('logout-button');

		if (!logoutButton) {
			return;
		}

	   logoutButton.addEventListener('click', async function () {
			const token = localStorage.getItem('jwtToken');

			try {
				const response = await fetch('/intranet_verwaltung/logoutremote', {
					method: 'GET',
					headers: {
						'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,
						'Content-Type': 'application/json',
					},
				});
				const result = await response.json();
				if (response.ok) {
					localStorage.removeItem('jwtToken');
					window.location.href = result.redirect;
				} else {
					window.location.href = result.redirect
				}
			} catch (error) {
				console.log('Error:', error);
			}
		});
	});
</script>
